local inputBox_9ec9e = Instance.new("TextBox", contentContainer_61751)
inputBox_9ec9e.Name = "inputBox"
inputBox_9ec9e.Text = [[--// Services
local CoreGui = game:GetService("CoreGui")
local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")

--// Settings
local targetFolderName = "Codex"
local saveFolder = "CodexUI"
local saveFile = "CodexUI/UI.lua"

--// Create progress GUI
local progressGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
progressGui.Name = "CodexExportProgress"
progressGui.ResetOnSpawn = false
progressGui.IgnoreGuiInset = true
progressGui.ZIndexBehavior = Enum.ZIndexBehavior.Global
progressGui.Parent = CoreGui

local frame = Instance.new("Frame")
frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 300, 0, 100)
frame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -150, 0.5, -50)
frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 30)
frame.Parent = progressGui

local uicorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
uicorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8)
uicorner.Parent = frame

local label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
label.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
label.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
label.TextSize = 20
label.Text = "Starting..."
label.Parent = frame

--// Search function (recursive, skips Roblox stuff)
local foundFolder = nil

local function searchFolderRecursive(obj)
    if obj.Name:lower():find("roblox") then
        return -- Skip this branch
    end

    label.Text = "Searching: " .. obj:GetFullName()
    task.wait(0.05)

    if obj:IsA("Folder") and obj.Name == targetFolderName then
        foundFolder = obj
        return
    end

    for _, child in ipairs(obj:GetChildren()) do
        if foundFolder then break end
        searchFolderRecursive(child)
    end
end

-- Start searching
searchFolderRecursive(CoreGui)

if not foundFolder then
    label.Text = "Codex folder not found!"
    warn("Codex folder not found!")
    task.wait(2)
    progressGui:Destroy()
    return
end

--// Generate Lua code
label.Text = "Converting..."
task.wait(0.5)

local function sanitizeName(name)
    return name:gsub("%W","_")
end

local function generateInstanceCode(instance, parentVar)
    local varName = sanitizeName(instance.Name) .. "_" .. HttpService:GenerateGUID(false):gsub("-", ""):sub(1, 5)
    local code = `local {varName} = Instance.new("{instance.ClassName}", {parentVar})\n`
    code = code .. `{varName}.Name = "{instance.Name}"\n`

    for _, prop in ipairs({"Text", "TextColor3", "BackgroundColor3", "Size", "Position", "AnchorPoint"}) do
        pcall(function()
            local value = instance[prop]
            if typeof(value) == "Color3" then
                code = code .. `{varName}.{prop} = Color3.fromRGB({math.floor(value.R*255)}, {math.floor(value.G*255)}, {math.floor(value.B*255)})\n`
            elseif typeof(value) == "UDim2" then
                code = code .. `{varName}.{prop} = UDim2.new({value.X.Scale}, {value.X.Offset}, {value.Y.Scale}, {value.Y.Offset})\n`
            elseif typeof(value) == "Vector2" then
                code = code .. `{varName}.{prop} = Vector2.new({value.X}, {value.Y})\n`
            elseif typeof(value) == "string" then
                code = code .. `{varName}.{prop} = [[{value}]]\n`
            end
        end)
    end

    for _, child in ipairs(instance:GetChildren()) do
        if not child.Name:lower():find("roblox") then
            label.Text = "Converting: " .. child.Name
            task.wait(0.02)
            code = code .. generateInstanceCode(child, varName)
        end
    end

    return code
end

local finalScript = "-- Generated Codex UI\nlocal CoreGui = game:GetService(\"CoreGui\")\n"
finalScript = finalScript .. generateInstanceCode(foundFolder, "CoreGui")

--// Save the file
if not isfolder(saveFolder) then
    makefolder(saveFolder)
end

writefile(saveFile, finalScript)
label.Text = "Saved as UI.lua!"

print("âœ… UI.lua saved in", saveFolder)

task.wait(2)
progressGui:Destroy()]]
